 Sure thing! Here is a potential stress-at-workquestionaire:
```vbnet
1) In general, how often do you feel stressed while performing job duties? (Always / Often / Sometimes / Rarely or Never ) 	2). How would YOU define "stress"? Is it just an emotional state that can be easily dismissed and ignored OR is stress a sign of something more serious to which attention should paid promptly
3) Have you ever felt physically ill as resultant from work-related pressures? (Yes / No ) 	4). How do YOU feel about the amount/levels or resources available at your workplace for managing pressure and preventing burnout in employees, including yourself: Enough OR Lacking ?  5. In past few months how many times you have thought of leaving this job due to stress? (0-1 / 2 -3 // More than Three)
6). How do YOU feel about the level/amounts or support from your superiors and colleagues in terms managing pressure, preventing burnout: Enough OR Lacking ?  7. Do you have a tendency of blaming other people for problems at work? (Yes / No ) 8 . On scale to one-ten where ten is high do YOU feel that management understands the importance or impact stress can cause on employees and their performance
9). How often are your targets set realistically, considering YOUR abilities as employee: Always/Often//Sometimes // Rarely?  10. Have you ever received support from HR department regarding work-related pressures (Yes / No ) 	    And finally... Is there anything else YOU would like to share or add about stress at your workplace and how it could be better managed ?
```Please let me know if this questionnaire meets the needs of user, otherwise I can make some changes.

This is a JSON object that represents a survey about the effectiveness of employee training programs. The survey contains 7 questions, each with a unique code, display order, and set of possible answers. The questions are displayed as a set of radio buttons, and the user can select only one answer per question.

The first question is a rating of overall satisfaction with the training programs, with possible answers ranging from "Extremely Unsatisfied" to "Very Satisfied". The second question asks whether learning objectives were met for each specific course, with possible answers of "Yes" or "No". The third question asks how well the materials presented in training sessions translated into real-life application and performance improvement, with possible answers ranging from "Very well" to "Very poorly". The fourth question asks if there is enough time allocated between trainings for participants to absorb all information properly, with possible answers of "Yes" or "No". The fifth question asks if the methods used in delivering training sessions have been effective for retention and recall of knowledge, with possible answers of "Yes" or "No". The sixth question asks if it is easy or difficult to measure impact on employees' performance, productivity after a specific course has taken place, with possible answers ranging from "Very easy" to "Very difficult". The seventh and final question asks if the company provides enough opportunities to learn new skills through trainings, with possible answers of "Yes" or "No".

The questions in this survey can help an organization understand the effectiveness of its employee training programs and identify areas for improvement. By collecting and analyzing survey responses, an organization can gather valuable insights about the strengths and weaknesses of its training programs and make data-driven decisions about how to improve them.

This questionnaire has been designed for both exempt (salaried) employees as well non managers in order capture more comprehensive picture employee experience at our organization:
1 **On scale 0-5, how would you rate your overall job satisfaction?** Please select the first number that comes into mind and do not spend too much time thinking. This will help us understand if people generally feel satisfied or dissatisfied with their work situation on average across all employees surveyed2 How often are able to take breaks when needed during working day – never, rarely sometimes frequently very frequent?
3 **Do you have enough autonomy and flexibility in your job role** that allows for creativity innovation problem-solving thinking outside the box or do managers strictly enforce specific procedures without room negotiation input ideas from team members about how things could be improved. Please answer on scale 0 to15 where zero means no control whatsoever over work life, and fifteen meaning complete autonomy?
4 **On a seven-point Likert Scale (where one is strongly disagree two moderately disagrees three slightly disagree four neither agree nor**disage five slight agreement six moderate agreements or 7 completely agrees), please rate the following statement: "I feel like I am able to balance my work and personal life effectively."
5 **Do you have access resources tools technology equipment needed perform job at highest level? Yes no if yes, would it be possible for us provide more specific information about what types of technologies or other items might help make your tasks easier. If not please explain why in detail so we can address any potential issues quickly and efficiently.**
6 **On a scale 0-15 where zero means never have occasion to give feedback on work performance, five is average frequency six seven eight nine ten eleven twelve thirteen fourteen fifteen sixteen seventeen eighteen nineteen twenty**twenty one or Twenty two times per year for example if person has been with company more than three months and works closely under supervision management team members who are able evaluate their own job skills abilities through observations during daily activities, please rate the following statement: "I feel comfortable giving constructive feedback on work performance."
7 **Do you think our organization values its employees? Yes no if yes explain why or give specific examples of how this value has been demonstrated in your experience. If not possible provide reasons for feeling undervalued.** 8 How often do managers initiate one-onone meetings with team members (never, rarely sometimes frequently very frequent)?
9 **On a scale from zero to ten where five is neutral and anything above that means positive how would you rate our company culture?** Please explain answer in detail if possible. For example: "I feel like there's open communication between departments which fosters sense of community" or something similar so we can understand what aspects contribute towards making people enjoy working here more than others might not have same opinion
10 **Do you agree with our company values and mission statement? Yes no if yes, please elaborate on why. If No explain in detail how those things could be improved** 5 How often do managers actively seek employee input into decision-making processes (never rarely sometimes frequently very frequent)?

```python
1) How would you rate overall availability (both in-person training sessions or online resources)?  	Extremely available, Available upon request but not always quickly enough so occasionally have to wait a little bit before getting what I need.  Not very accessible at all - feel like technology is only for certain people and that's definitely NOT me!
2) How easy it was/is finding information about how different tools work together (for example, if you can use one tool as an input into another)?  	Very difficult because there are so many options out in the market.  It feels like everything works with something else but just don't know where to start or what is best practice!
3) How satisfied were/are employees when they first started using specific tools, considering their previous experience?    Extremely - even if initially not very comfortable because of a steep learning curve associated.  Not at all; found it hard and still struggle with certain toolset due to lack in training or support materials available
4) What do you think about the accessibility for people who have disabilities, including those related specifically through technology?  	Very accessible - everything has been designed keeping everyone's needs into account.  Not very much; not enough thought given beyond compliance with legal minimum standards which makes it difficult to use these tools
5) Can employees get training on how certain technologies work and why they should be using them in their jobs (for example, if someone wants a tutorial about Microsoft Office)?  	Yes - always provided when requested.  No; not even once did I receive any kind of formal or informal education regarding this toolset
6) Is there an easy way to provide feedback on the technology tools currently being used by employees?    Absolutely! There are multiple channels including online form, email address and other avenues that make it simple.  Not really; would like more opportunities for constructive criticism without feeling guilty about doing so because of potential pushback from management
7) How do you feel when using technology tools in your job (for example: if they're slow or not user-friendly)?  	Very comfortable and empowered, able to get things done quickly.  Frustrated; it feels like there are too many clicks required just for basic tasks which makes me less productive than I could be
8) Is the technology easy enough that you can use without help from someone else?    Yes - very intuitive user interface and simple navigation make this possible!   No, not really.  Need constant support to navigate through different platforms due in part because of poor design choices made by developers/managers responsible for these tools
9) Have employees been able access all the technology they need or do some still struggle with certain things?    Yes - have everything necessary at my fingertips!   No, not always.  Sometimes feel like there is a missing tool preventing me from performing optimally in role and job responsibilities demand that I find solution
10) Can you share your thoughts about how technology can be made more accessible for everyone within the company?    Sure thing - would love to see universal design principles incorporated throughout all aspects of our organization.  Not sure if this is possible but definitely think we could do better than current state by focusing on usability and accessibility as key drivers in decision-making process

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a potentialquestionaireonInternalMobiiltyOpportunties:
```vbnet
1) How long have you been with this company? ________. That's great, because it means we can tap into your wealth of experience and knowledge about the organization. 🌿Do you feel like internal mobility opportunities are available to all employees equally or do certain people seem "stuck" in their roles due only external factors such as budget constraints?
2) Have YOU ever had a chance for aninternal move during YOUR tenure with this company, and if yes – how did it go overall (both positives AND negatives)? If not - what reasons can you think of that might be preventing internal mobility from happening more often at our workplace 🤓?
3) According to YOU: How important is a strong cultural fit between an employee wantingto move internally and the team they would potentially join (on scale1-5, where one means "notimportant"and five - extremely)? And what about technical skills match – how crucial it can be for someone's success in new role?
4) When we talk specific numbers: What % of internal mobility cases are initiated by employees themselves vs. management/HR team (according to YOUR knowledge and experience with the company 📊)?; Do you think self-nomination is a good thing or should be encouraged more, because people know THEMSELVES best?
5) In your opinion: How can we make internal mobility process better for everyone involved - from giving feedback about unsuccessful cases to making sure there's no bad blood between teams after someone leaves (and what would YOU do if given a chance)? 🌱; And how often should such opportunities be available, according To YOUR PERSONAL preference?
6) Can you tell me moreabout the training process for internal moves – is it thorough enough and tailored to each person's needs or just basic onboarding with no specific growth plan (and why do YOU think so)? 🌞; Is there a way we could improve this aspect, making sure people are well-prepared when starting their new role?
7) According To YOUR OBSERVATIONS: How much does turnover rate affect internal mobility opportunities – if it's high then probably not enough time/resources for everyone to get proper training and tools needed. And how can we make this situation better by reducing the overall attrition in company 🌪?
8) Finally, do YOU think that people should be ableto move freely within acompany without any restrictions based on job title or level (assuming they have necessary skills)? [LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is an example kick off meeting feedback survey:
```vbnet
1) How would you rate this year's virtual format for our annual company wide meetup? (5 point scale, with 4 being "neutral" and higher numbers indicating a more positive rating.) Did it feel like the benefits of in-person communication were preserved to some degree through technology or not really.
2) How would you rate this year's meeting agenda for our kick off session ? Was there appropriate time dedicated towards team building, goal setting & vision casting? Or did we focus too much on operational details and logistics that could have been covered in a different way without taking up as many precious minutes of your life.
3) How would you rate the content presented during this year's kick off meeting ? Was it relevant to everyone or was there an uneven distribution where certain topics felt more important than others? Did we strike balance between business and personal that is so essential for a successful company culture, Or did some things feel out of whack.
4) How would you rate the overall flow & pacing during this year's kick off meeting ? Was it well organized or chaotic with too many distractions taking away from main content? Did we leave enough time at end to ask questions and provide feedback, Or did that get lost in shuffle of things.
5) How would you rate the selection & use technology tools during this year's kick off meeting ? Were they appropriate for purpose or not really useful because something was missing which could have made all difference . Did we strike balance between human interaction elements and technological features, Or did some people feel like just another number in big sea of names.
6) How would you rate the level communication during this year's kick off meeting ? Was it clear enough or were there miscommunications that led to confusion? Were participants able speak up easily when they wanted without feeling intimidated by power dynamics, Or did some people feel like their voices weren’t heard and things got lost in translation.
7) How would you rate the effectiveness of this year's kick off meeting as a way for us all connect with each other ? Did it help build stronger relationships or was there an awkwardness that made everyone uncomfortable? Were we able to see beyond just words, into people behind those messages and felt closer together in spite distance.
8) How would you rate the overall success of this year's kick off meeting on scale 1-5 with five being very successful ? If so why if not then what could have been done better? And finally how can we improve going forward based upon your feedback that will help us make next time even more productive and enjoyable for all.
```
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Kick-off Meeting Feedback

3. How often have you observed positive interactions between people of different races and ethnicities in your organization? (Always, Often , Sometimes / Rarely ; Never )4). Do employees from marginalized groups participate actively during discussions about diversity issues or feel that their opinions are respected by others after taking this training course ?
5. How many diverse candidates were interviewed for open positions before implementing the program and how does it compare to current numbers? (More than 70% , Between  41-69%; Less then / equal To   32%) . Also, what is your opinion about number of minorities in leadership roles within company ?
(Too few; Just right ; Too many)	5. Is there any difference between the level and quality Of interactions with people from different racial/ethnic backgrounds before vs after training course? (Strongly disagree , Disagree, Neutral / not sure  AgREE or StrongLY agree )

8 . Does this program help you to understand how certain policies/practices within your organization may unintentionally exclude people based on their race and ethnicity ?	9. (Strongly disagree , Disagree, Neutral / not sure  AgREE or StrongLY agree)
10 . Do you think this program is successful in helping employees to recognize and challenge their own stereotypes ? 12. Has there been a noticeable increase in number and quality 	of interpersonal relationships between employees after taking this diversity program ? (Strongly disagree , Disagree; Neutral / not sure ; AgREE OR StrongLY agree)

7) Are you satisfied with your current communication technology for smartworking? (select all the apply): __communication_satisfaction__ %%[Multiple choice, not anonymous]{.mc} - Yes   ________    >!|     |      <-----PLEASE SELECT---------- 	- No

```Please note that some questions allow multiple choices and others do only one answer per question (multiple or single). The technology used for communication is not anonymous. Each question in the "_TF\_QUESTIONS" array has the following properties:

* "TYPE\_ID": (int) the question's type.
* "DISPLAY\_ORDER": (int) the question's display order.
* "_TF\_ANSWERS": An array of objects, each representing a possible answer to the question.

Each answer object in the "_TF\_ANSWERS" array has a single property "ANSWER", which is a string representing the content of the answer.

The admitted question's types are the following:

* ID: 1, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose one answer from a list.
* ID: 2, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to choose more than one answer from a list.
* ID: 3, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rate something on a scale.
* ID: 4, DESCRIPTION: Use this type of question to rank something.

 Sure thing! Here is one possible version for a work load management survey:
```vbnet
1) Do you feel like there are too many tasks assigned in comparison with available resources? (Multiple Choice, Yes or No questions encouraged to get more precise information!) 🔌🤔👍🏽‍♂️. If yes what is your opinion on the ideal number of projects that can be handled by one person at a time??
2) How often do you work overtime and why: Is it due-to external factors or internal company processes? (Multiple Choice, Yes/No Questions encouraged to get more precise information!) 🔌🤔👍🏽‍♂️. If yes what is your opinion on the ideal number of projects that can be handled by one person at a time??
3) Do you feel like there are too many tasks assigned in comparison with available resources? (Multiple Choice, Yes or No questions encouraged to get more precise information!) 🔌🤔👍🏽‍♂️. If yes what is your opinion on the ideal number of projects that can be handled by one person at a time??
4) How do you prioritize tasks and why: Is it based off urgency, importance or some other method? (Multiple Choice questions encouraged to get more precise information!) 🔌🤔👍🏽‍♂️. If yes what is your opinion on the ideal number of projects that can be handled by one person at a time??
5) Have you tried any workload management techniques and which ones were most helpful for balancing tasks? (Multiple Choice questions encouraged to get more precise information!) 🔌🤔👍🏽‍♂️. If yes what is your opinion on the ideal number of projects that can be handled by one person at a time??
6) Do you think there are enough resources available in terms staffing and technology for workload management? (Multiple Choice, Yes or No questions encouraged to get more precise information!) 🔌🤔👍🏽‍♂️. If no what would make the situation better: More people/technology perhaps??
7) How do you handle unplanned tasks that arise without warning and how much time is devoted towards these? (Multiple Choice, Yes or No questions encouraged to get more precise information!) 🔌🤔👍🏽‍♂️. If yes what would make the situation better: More people/technology perhaps??
8) Have you tried any workload management techniques for unplanned tasks and which ones were most helpful? (Multiple Choice, Yes or No questions encouraged to get more precise information!) 🔌🤔👍🏽‍♂️. If yes what is your opinion on the ideal number of projects that can be handled by one person at a time??
9) Do you think there are enough resources available in terms staffing and technology for workload management? (Multiple Choice, Yes or No questions encouraged to get more precise information!) 🔌🤔👍🏽‍♂️. If no what would make the situation better: More people/technology perhaps??
10) Do you feel like your current role is fulfillling with a sense of accomplishment and pride? (Multiple Choice, Yes or No questions encouraged to get more precise information!) 🔌🤔👍🏽‍♂️. If no what would make the situation better: More people/technology perhaps??
